### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Arquitetura e Repositório Base

## Arquitetura V10 - Decisões Técnicas

### ADR-001: Stack Tecnológica Principal
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**CONTEXTO:**
Precisamos definir uma stack tecnológica moderna, sustentável e com forte ecossistema para suportar 100% de autonomia e estabilidade. A stack anterior era heterogênea e difícil de manter.

**DECISÃO:**
- **Frontend:** React 18 + TypeScript + Vite
- **Backend:** Node.js 20 + Express + TypeScript
- **Banco de Dados:** PostgreSQL (produção) + SQLite (desenvolvimento/testes)
- **Cache:** Redis
- **Fila de Mensagens:** RabbitMQ
- **Containerização:** Docker + Docker Compose
- **Orquestração:** Kubernetes (para produção)
- **Monitoramento:** Prometheus + Grafana + ELK Stack

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A (React/Node.js):** Prós: Ecossistema vasto, comunidade ativa, TypeScript nativo. Contras: JavaScript runtime.
- **Opção B (Vue/Go):** Prós: Performance excelente, tipagem forte. Contras: Curva de aprendizado, ecossistema menor.
- **Escolhida: A** - Justificativa: Maior produtividade da squad, facilidade de contratação, suporte a TypeScript em toda stack.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
- Positivas: Desenvolvimento rápido, ampla documentação, fácil integração com ferramentas de IA
- Negativas: Necessidade de otimização de performance em Node.js
- Riscos: Vulnerabilidades em pacotes NPM - mitigação com dependabot e auditoria semanal

### ADR-002: Estrutura de Pastas
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead

**DECISÃO:**
Estrutura monorepo com workspaces para frontend, backend e shared:
```
diyapp-v10/
├── .github/
│   ├── workflows/
│   └── dependabot.yml
├── apps/
│   ├── frontend/
│   └── backend/
├── packages/
│   ├── shared/
│   ├── types/
│   └── ui/
├── infrastructure/
├── scripts/
└── docs/
```

---

## REPOSITÓRIO BASE COMPLETO

### 1. Estrutura de Arquivos

```bash
# Criando estrutura de pastas
mkdir -p diyapp-v10/{.github/workflows,apps/{frontend/src,backend/src},packages/{shared/src,types/src,ui/src},infrastructure/{k8s,docker},scripts,docs/adrs}
```

### 2. Arquivos de Configuração Raiz

**package.json** (monorepo):
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v10",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "private": true,
  "workspaces": [
    "apps/*",
    "packages/*"
  ],
  "scripts": {
    "dev": "concurrently \"npm run dev:backend\" \"npm run dev:frontend\"",
    "dev:backend": "npm run dev --workspace=backend",
    "dev:frontend": "npm run dev --workspace=frontend",
    "build": "npm run build --workspaces",
    "test": "npm run test --workspaces",
    "lint": "npm run lint --workspaces",
    "format": "prettier --write .",
    "docker:up": "docker-compose up -d",
    "docker:down": "docker-compose down",
    "prepare": "husky install"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "concurrently": "^8.2.2",
    "husky": "^8.0.3",
    "lint-staged": "^15.2.0",
    "prettier": "^3.1.1"
  },
  "engines": {
    "node": ">=20.0.0",
    "npm": ">=10.0.0"
  }
}
```

### 3. Configuração CI/CD

**.github/workflows/ci.yml**:
```yaml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  lint-and-test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    strategy:
      matrix:
        node-version: [20.x]

    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Use Node.js ${{ matrix.node-version }}
      uses: actions/setup-node@v4
      with:
        node-version: ${{ matrix.node-version }}
        cache: 'npm'
    
    - name: Install Dependencies
      run: npm ci
    
    - name: Lint
      run: npm run lint
    
    - name: Test
      run: npm run test
    
    - name: Build
      run: npm run build

  security-scan:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint-and-test
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Run Snyk to check for vulnerabilities
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Run CodeQL Analysis
      uses: github/codeql-action/analyze@v3

  docker-build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: security-scan
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
    
    - name: Login to DockerHub
      uses: docker/login-action@v3
      with:
        username: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}
        password: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_PASSWORD }}
    
    - name: Build and push backend
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
      with:
        context: ./apps/backend
        push: true
        tags: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/diyapp-backend:latest
    
    - name: Build and push frontend
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
      with:
        context: ./apps/frontend
        push: true
        tags: ${{ secrets.DOCKER_USERNAME }}/diyapp-frontend:latest
```

**.github/workflows/cd.yml**:
```yaml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["CI Pipeline"]
    branches: [main]
    types:
      - completed

jobs:
  deploy:
    if: ${{ github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success' }}
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    
    steps:
    - name: Checkout
      uses: actions/checkout@v4
    
    - name: Deploy to Kubernetes
      env:
        KUBECONFIG: ${{ secrets.KUBECONFIG }}
      run: |
        kubectl apply -f infrastructure/k8s/
        kubectl rollout status deployment/diyapp-backend
        kubectl rollout status deployment/diyapp-frontend
    
    - name: Run Smoke Tests
      run: |
        ./scripts/smoke-test.sh
```

**.github/dependabot.yml**:
```yaml
version: 2
updates:
  - package-ecosystem: "npm"
    directory: "/"
    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"
    open-pull-requests-limit: 10
    reviewers:
      - "tech-lead"
    labels:
      - "dependencies"
      - "security"

  - package-ecosystem: "docker"
    directory: "/"
    schedule:
      interval: "weekly"
```

### 4. Docker Configuration

**docker-compose.yml**:
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp_dev
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3.12-management-alpine
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: diyapp
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: diyapp_dev
    ports:
      - "5672:5672"
      - "15672:15672"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  backend:
    build:
      context: ./apps/backend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:diyapp_dev@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      RABBITMQ_URL: amqp://diyapp:diyapp_dev@rabbitmq:5672
    volumes:
      - ./apps/backend:/app
      - /app/node_modules
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy

  frontend:
    build:
      context: ./apps/frontend
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./apps/frontend:/app
      - /app/node_modules
    depends_on:
      - backend

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

**apps/backend/src/index.ts** (Ponto de entrada):
```typescript
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import compression from 'compression';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import { createServer } from 'http';
import { config } from './config';
import { logger } from './utils/logger';
import { errorHandler } from './middlewares/errorHandler';
import { requestLogger } from './middlewares/requestLogger';
import { healthRouter } from './routes/health';
import { apiRouter } from './routes/api';

const app = express();
const server = createServer(app);

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors(config.cors));
app.use(compression());

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.'
});
app.use('/api', limiter);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Request logging
app.use(requestLogger);

// Routes
app.use('/health', healthRouter);
app.use('/api/v1', apiRouter);

// Swagger documentation
if (config.env === 'development') {
  const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');
  const swaggerSpec = require('./swagger');
  app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerSpec));
}

// 404 handler
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.path}`
  });
});

// Error handling
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start server
server.listen(config.port, () => {
  logger.info(`Server running on port ${config.port} in ${config.env} mode`);
  logger.info(`API Documentation available at http://localhost:${config.port}/api-docs`);
});

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
  server.close(() => {
    logger.info('Server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

export { app, server };
```

**apps/backend/src/config/index.ts**:
```typescript
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const configSchema = z.object({
  env: z.enum(['development', 'test', 'production']).default('development'),
  port: z.coerce.number().default(3001),
  database: z.object({
    url: z.string().url(),
    pool: z.object({
      min: z.coerce.number().default(2),
      max: z.coerce.number().default(10)
    })
  }),
  redis: z.object({
    url: z.string().url()
  }),
  rabbitmq: z.object({
    url: z.string().url()
  }),
  jwt

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core - Design System

Vou criar um Design System completo e funcional para o DIYAPP V10, com foco em acessibilidade, componentes reutilizáveis e wireframes de alta fidelidade para todas as views principais.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v10-design-system/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── style.css              # Estilos do Design System
├── design-system.html     # Documentação do Design System
├── components.js          # Componentes JavaScript
├── views/                 # Wireframes de alta fidelidade
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── agent-creation.html
│   ├── logs.html
│   └── settings.html
├── assets/
│   ├── fonts/
│   ├── icons/
│   └── images/
└── README.md
```

// 5. src/store/appStore.ts
import { create } from 'zustand';
import { persist } from 'zustand/middleware';

export type AgentStatus = 'active' | 'inactive' | 'error' | 'loading';

export interface Agent {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  description: string;
  status: AgentStatus;
  lastActive: string;
  performance: number; // 0-100
  tasksCompleted: number;
}

export interface AppState {
  // Agents state
  agents: Agent[];
  selectedAgentId: string | null;
  
  // UI state
  sidebarCollapsed: boolean;
  darkMode: boolean;
  isLoading: boolean;
  
  // Actions
  setAgents: (agents: Agent[]) => void;
  addAgent: (agent: Agent) => void;
  updateAgent: (id: string, updates: Partial<Agent>) => void;
  deleteAgent: (id: string) => void;
  selectAgent: (id: string | null) => void;
  toggleSidebar: () => void;
  toggleDarkMode: () => void;
  setLoading: (loading: boolean) => void;
}

export const useAppStore = create<AppState>()(
  persist(
    (set) => ({
      // Initial state
      agents: [
        {
          id: '1',
          name: 'Dev Frontend',
          description: 'Implementa interfaces com fidelidade ao design',
          status: 'active',
          lastActive: '2024-01-15T10:30:00Z',
          performance: 95,
          tasksCompleted: 42,
        },
        {
          id: '2',
          name: 'Dev Backend',
          description: 'Gerencia APIs e lógica de negócio',
          status: 'active',
          lastActive: '2024-01-15T09:45:00Z',
          performance: 88,
          tasksCompleted: 38,
        },
        {
          id: '3',
          name: 'UX Designer',
          description: 'Cria especificações de design e protótipos',
          status: 'inactive',
          lastActive: '2024-01-14T16:20:00Z',
          performance: 92,
          tasksCompleted: 27,
        },
      ],
      selectedAgentId: null,
      sidebarCollapsed: false,
      darkMode: false,
      isLoading: false,
      
      // Actions implementation
      setAgents: (agents) => set({ agents }),
      addAgent: (agent) => set((state) => ({ agents: [...state.agents, agent] })),
      updateAgent: (id, updates) =>
        set((state) => ({
          agents: state.agents.map((agent) =>
            agent.id === id ? { ...agent, ...updates } : agent
          ),
        })),
      deleteAgent: (id) =>
        set((state) => ({
          agents: state.agents.filter((agent) => agent.id !== id),
          selectedAgentId: state.selectedAgentId === id ? null : state.selectedAgentId,
        })),
      selectAgent: (id) => set({ selectedAgentId: id }),
      toggleSidebar: () => set((state) => ({ sidebarCollapsed: !state.sidebarCollapsed })),
      toggleDarkMode: () => set((state) => ({ darkMode: !state.darkMode })),
      setLoading: (loading) => set({ isLoading: loading }),
    }),
    {
      name: 'diyapp-storage',
      partialize: (state) => ({
        sidebarCollapsed: state.sidebarCollapsed,
        darkMode: state.darkMode,
      }),
    }
  )
);

// 6. src/components/layout/Header.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { Menu, Bell, Search, User } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAppStore } from '../../store/appStore';
import { Button } from '../ui/Button';

interface HeaderProps {
  onMenuClick?: () => void;
}

export const Header: React.FC<HeaderProps> = ({ onMenuClick }) => {
  const { toggleSidebar, sidebarCollapsed } = useAppStore();
  
  const handleMenuClick = () => {
    toggleSidebar();
    onMenuClick?.();
  };
  
  return (
    <header 
      className="header"
      role="banner"
      aria-label="Cabeçalho principal"
    >
      <div className="header-container">
        {/* Left section */}
        <div className="header-left">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            onClick={handleMenuClick}
            aria-label={sidebarCollapsed ? 'Expandir menu' : 'Recolher menu'}
            aria-expanded={!sidebarCollapsed}
          >
            <Menu size={20} />
          </Button>
          
          <div className="header-logo">
            <span className="logo-text">DIYAPP</span>
            <span className="logo-version">Evolution V10</span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Center section - Search */}
        <div className="header-center">
          <div className="search-container">
            <Search 
              className="search-icon" 
              size={18} 
              aria-hidden="true"
            />
            <input
              type="search"
              className="search-input"
              placeholder="Buscar agentes, tarefas..."
              aria-label="Buscar no sistema"
            />
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Right section */}
        <div className="header-right">
          <Button
            variant="ghost"
            size="icon"
            aria-label="Notificações"
            aria-describedby="notification-count"
          >
            <Bell

```javascript
// src/server.js
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const logger = require('./config/logger');
const { errorHandler } = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const { requestLogger } = require('./middleware/requestLogger');
const healthRoutes = require('./routes/health.routes');
const agentRoutes = require('./routes/agent.routes');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());

// CORS configuration
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || 'http://localhost:8080',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting for public endpoints
const publicLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: { error: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});

// Body parsing middleware
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10kb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10kb' }));

// Request logging middleware
app.use(requestLogger);

// Routes
app.use('/api/v1/health', publicLimiter, healthRoutes);
app.use('/api/v1/agents', agentRoutes);

// 404 handler
app.use('*', (req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.originalUrl}`
  });
});

// Global error handler
app.use(errorHandler);

// Start server
const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`Server running on port ${PORT}`);
  logger.info(`Environment: ${process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development'}`);
});

// Graceful shutdown
process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
  logger.info('SIGTERM received. Shutting down gracefully...');
  server.close(() => {
    logger.info('Server closed. Process terminated.');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  logger.info('SIGINT received. Shutting down gracefully...');
  server.close(() => {
    logger.info('Server closed. Process terminated.');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

module.exports = { app, server };
```

```javascript
// src/config/logger.js
const winston = require('winston');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v10-core' },
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/error.log', 
      level: 'error',
      maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
      maxFiles: 5
    }),
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: 'logs/combined.log',
      maxsize: 5242880,
      maxFiles: 5
    })
  ]
});

// Console transport for non-production environments
if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize(),
      winston.format.simple()
    )
  }));
}

// Mask sensitive data in logs
logger.addMask = (data) => {
  if (typeof data !== 'object') return data;
  
  const masked = { ...data };
  const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'apiKey', 'secret', 'email', 'cpf', 'creditCard'];
  
  sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
    if (masked[field]) {
      masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return masked;
};

module.exports = logger;
```

```javascript
// src/config/database.js
const sqlite3 = require('sqlite3').verbose();
const path = require('path');
const logger = require('./logger');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.db = null;
    this.initPromise = null;
  }

  async init() {
    if (this.initPromise) return this.initPromise;

    this.initPromise = new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const dbPath = process.env.DB_PATH || path.join(__dirname, '..', '..', 'database.sqlite');
      
      this.db = new sqlite3.Database(dbPath, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Failed to connect to database:', err);
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        
        logger.info(`Connected to SQLite database at ${dbPath}`);
        
        // Enable foreign keys
        this.db.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON');
        
        // Create tables
        this.createTables()
          .then(() => {
            logger.info('Database tables created/verified');
            resolve();
          })
          .catch(reject);
      });
    });

    return this.initPromise;
  }

  async createTables() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const agentsTable = `
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agents (
          id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
          name TEXT NOT NULL,
          role TEXT NOT NULL,
          status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
          config JSON,
          created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          updated_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          version INTEGER DEFAULT 1
        )
      `;

      const agentMetricsTable = `
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agent_metrics (
          id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
          agent_id TEXT NOT NULL,
          metric_type TEXT NOT NULL,
          value REAL NOT NULL,
          recorded_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
          FOREIGN KEY (agent_id) REFERENCES agents(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
        )
      `;

      this.db.serialize(() => {
        this.db.run(agentsTable, (err) => {
          if (err) {
            reject(err);
            return;
          }
        });

        this.db.run(agentMetricsTable, (err) => {
          if (err) {
            reject(err);
            return;
          }
        });

        // Create indexes
        this.db.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_agents_status ON agents(status)');
        this.db.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_agent_metrics_agent_id ON agent_metrics(agent_id)');
        this.db.run('CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_agent_metrics_recorded_at ON agent_metrics(recorded_at)');

        resolve();
      });
    });
  }

  async query(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.all(sql, params, (err, rows) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database query error:', { sql, params, error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve(rows);
      });
    });
  }

  async run(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.run(sql, params, function(err) {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database run error:', { sql, params, error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve({ lastID: this.lastID, changes: this.changes });
      });
    });
  }

  async get(sql, params = []) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.get(sql, params, (err, row) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Database get error:', { sql, params, error: err.message });
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        resolve(row);
      });
    });
  }

  async close() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.db.close((err) => {
        if (err) {
          logger.error('Failed to close database:', err);
          reject(err);
          return;
        }
        logger.info('Database connection closed');
        resolve();
      });
    });
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const database = new Database();

module.exports = database;
```

```javascript
// src/models/agent.model.js
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const database = require('../config/database');
const logger = require('../config/logger');

class AgentModel {
  constructor() {
    this.tableName = 'agents';
  }

  async create(agentData) {
    const id = uuidv4();
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    
    const agent = {
      id,
      name: agentData.name,
      role: agentData.role,
      status: agentData.status || 'active',
      config: JSON.stringify(agentData.config || {}),
      created_at: now,
      updated_at: now,
      version: 1
    };

    const sql = `
      INSERT INTO ${this.tableName} 
      (id, name, role, status, config, created_at, updated_at, version)
      VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
    `;

    const params = [
      agent.id,
      agent.name,
      agent.role,
      agent.status,
      agent.config,
      agent.created_at,
      agent.updated_at,
      agent.version
    ];

    try {
      await database.run(sql, params);
      return { ...agent, config: JSON.parse(agent.config) };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to create agent:', { agentData: logger.addMask(agentData), error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async findById(id) {
    const sql = `SELECT * FROM ${this.tableName} WHERE id = ?`;
    
    try {
      const row = await database.get(sql, [id]);
      if (!row) return null;
      
      return {
        ...row,
        config: row.config ? JSON.parse(row.config) : {}
      };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to find agent by ID:', { id, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async findAll(filters = {}) {
    let sql = `SELECT * FROM ${this.tableName}`;
    const params = [];
    const conditions = [];

    if (filters.status) {
      conditions.push('status = ?');
      params.push(filters.status);
    }

    if (filters.role) {
      conditions.push('role = ?');
      params.push(filters.role);
    }

    if (conditions.length > 0) {
      sql += ' WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ');
    }

    sql += ' ORDER BY created_at DESC';

    if (filters.limit) {
      sql += ' LIMIT ?';
      params.push(filters.limit);
    }

    if (filters.offset) {
      sql += ' OFFSET ?';
      params.push(filters.offset);
    }

    try {
      const rows = await database.query(sql, params);
      return rows.map(row => ({
        ...row,
        config: row.config ? JSON.parse(row.config) : {}
      }));
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to find all agents:', { filters, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async update(id, updateData) {
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const currentAgent = await this.findById(id);
    
    if (!currentAgent) {
      return null;
    }

    const updates = [];
    const params = [];

    if (updateData.name !== undefined) {
      updates.push('name = ?');
      params.push(updateData.name);
    }

    if (updateData.role !== undefined) {
      updates.push('role = ?');
      params.push(updateData.role);
    }

    if (updateData.status !== undefined) {
      updates.push('status = ?');
      params.push(updateData.status);
    }

    if (updateData.config !== undefined) {
      updates.push('config = ?');
      params.push(JSON.stringify(updateData.config));
    }

    updates.push('updated_at = ?');
    params.push(now);

    updates.push('version = ?');
    params.push(currentAgent.version + 1);

    params.push(id);

    const sql = `
      UPDATE ${this.tableName} 
      SET ${updates.join(', ')}
      WHERE id = ?
    `;

    try {
      const result = await database.run(sql, params);
      if (result.changes === 0) {
        return null;
      }
      
      return await this.findById(id);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to update agent:', { id, updateData: logger.addMask(updateData), error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async delete(id) {
    const sql = `DELETE FROM ${this.tableName} WHERE id = ?`;
    
    try {
      const result = await database.run(sql, [id]);
      return result.changes > 0;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to delete agent:', { id, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async count(filters = {}) {
    let sql = `SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM ${this.tableName}`;
    const params = [];
    const conditions = [];

    if (filters.status) {
      conditions.push('status = ?');
      params.push(filters.status);
    }

    if (filters.role) {
      conditions.push('role = ?');
      params.push(filters.role);
    }

    if (conditions.length > 0) {
      sql += ' WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ');
    }

    try {
      const result = await database.get(sql, params);
      return result.count;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to count agents:', { filters, error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new AgentModel();
```

```javascript
// src/services/agent.service.js
const agentModel = require('../models/agent.model');
const logger = require('../config/logger');

class AgentService {
  async createAgent(agentData) {
    // Business logic validation
    if (!agentData.name || !agentData.role) {
      throw new Error('Name and role are required');
    }

    if (agentData.name.length > 100) {
      throw new Error('Name must be less than 100 characters');
    }

    // Check for duplicate names (business rule)
    const existingAgents = await agentModel.findAll({ name: agentData.name });
    if (existingAgents.length > 0) {
      throw new Error('Agent with this name already exists');
    }

    const agent = await agentModel.create(agentData);
    
    logger.info('Agent created successfully', { 
      agentId: agent.id,
      name: agent.name,
      role: agent.role 
    });

    return agent;
  }

  async getAgentById(id) {
    const agent = await agentModel.findById(id);
    
    if (!agent) {
      throw new Error('Agent not found');
    }

    return agent;
  }

  async getAllAgents(filters = {}) {
    const { page = 1, limit = 10, ...restFilters } = filters;
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

    const [agents, total] = await Promise.all([
      agentModel.findAll({ ...restFilters, limit, offset }),
      agentModel.count(restFilters)
    ]);

    return {
      agents,
      pagination: {
        page: parseInt(page),
        limit: parseInt(limit),
        total,
        pages: Math.ceil(total / limit)
      }
    };
  }

  async updateAgent(id, updateData) {
    // Business logic validation
    if (updateData.status && !['active', 'inactive', 'maintenance'].includes(updateData.status)) {
      throw new Error('Invalid status value');
    }

    const updatedAgent = await agentModel.update(id, updateData);
    
    if (!updatedAgent) {
      throw new Error('Agent not found');
    }

    logger.info('Agent updated successfully', { 
      agentId: id,
      updates: logger.addMask(updateData)
    });

    return updatedAgent;
  }

  async deleteAgent(id) {
    const deleted = await agentModel.delete(id);
    
    if (!deleted) {
      throw new Error('Agent not found');
    }

    logger.info('Agent deleted successfully', { agentId: id });

    return { success: true, message: 'Agent deleted successfully' };
  }

  async getAgentMetrics(id, period = '24h') {
    // This would integrate with a metrics service
    // For now, return basic metrics
    const agent = await this.getAgentById(id);
    
    return {
      agentId: id,
      name: agent.name,
      status: agent.status,
      metrics: {
        uptime: '99.9%',
        requests: 1500,
        errors: 2,
        avgResponseTime: 45
      },
      period
    };
  }
}

module.exports = new AgentService();
```

// src/controllers/agent.controller.js
const { validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const agentService = require('../services/agent.service');
const logger = require('../config/logger');

class AgentController {
  async

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V10 Core
-- Schema do Banco de Dados Principal
-- Data Engineer: Implementação inicial com migrações versionadas

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: agentes (entidade central do sistema)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agentes (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Identificação do agente
    nome VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    slug VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    versao VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1.0.0',
    
    -- Configuração do agente
    system_prompt TEXT NOT NULL,
    config JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Metadados de execução
    temperatura FLOAT DEFAULT 1.0,
    max_tokens INTEGER DEFAULT 2000,
    modelo VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT 'gpt-4',
    
    -- Status e controle
    ativo BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    modo_hive BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- Dados de criação e atualização
    criado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    atualizado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    criado_por VARCHAR(100),
    atualizado_por VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Indexes para performance
    CONSTRAINT check_temperatura CHECK (temperatura >= 0 AND temperatura <= 2),
    CONSTRAINT check_max_tokens CHECK (max_tokens > 0 AND max_tokens <= 100000)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_agentes_slug ON agentes(slug);
CREATE INDEX idx_agentes_ativo ON agentes(ativo);
CREATE INDEX idx_agentes_modo_hive ON agentes(modo_hive);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: logs_execucao (auditoria completa)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS logs_execucao (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Relacionamento com agente
    agente_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES agentes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Dados da execução
    entrada TEXT NOT NULL,
    saida TEXT,
    tokens_entrada INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    tokens_saida INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    custo_total DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Metadados de execução
    duracao_ms INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    erro TEXT,
    
    -- Contexto da execução
    contexto JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    sessao_id VARCHAR(100),
    usuario_id VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Timestamps
    iniciado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    finalizado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Indexes para queries frequentes
    CONSTRAINT check_status CHECK (status IN ('sucesso', 'erro', 'cancelado', 'pendente'))
);

CREATE INDEX idx_logs_agente_id ON logs_execucao(agente_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_iniciado_em ON logs_execucao(iniciado_em);
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_status ON logs_execucao(status);
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_sessao_id ON logs_execucao(sessao_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_usuario_id ON logs_execucao(usuario_id);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: configuracoes_sistema (configurações globais)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS configuracoes_sistema (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Chave única da configuração
    chave VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    valor JSONB NOT NULL,
    
    -- Metadados
    tipo VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'string',
    categoria VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'geral',
    descricao TEXT,
    
    -- Controle de acesso
    sensivel BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    editavel BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    
    -- Versionamento
    versao INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
    
    -- Timestamps
    criado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    atualizado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    atualizado_por VARCHAR(100),
    
    -- Validação
    CONSTRAINT check_tipo CHECK (tipo IN ('string', 'number', 'boolean', 'array', 'object'))
);

CREATE INDEX idx_config_chave ON configuracoes_sistema(chave);
CREATE INDEX idx_config_categoria ON configuracoes_sistema(categoria);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: migracoes (controle de versionamento do schema)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS migracoes (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Identificação da migração
    versao VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    nome VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    descricao TEXT,
    
    -- Status da migração
    aplicada BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    aplicada_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Checksum para validação
    checksum VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Timestamps
    criado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

CREATE INDEX idx_migracoes_versao ON migracoes(versao);
CREATE INDEX idx_migracoes_aplicada ON migracoes(aplicada);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: agentes_dependencias (relacionamentos entre agentes)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agentes_dependencias (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Relacionamento
    agente_origem_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES agentes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    agente_destino_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES agentes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Tipo de dependência
    tipo VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'chamada',
    
    -- Configuração da dependência
    config JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
    
    -- Ordem de execução
    ordem INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Timestamps
    criado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    UNIQUE(agente_origem_id, agente_destino_id, tipo),
    CONSTRAINT check_tipo_dependencia CHECK (tipo IN ('chamada', 'dados', 'evento', 'hierarquia'))
);

CREATE INDEX idx_deps_origem ON agentes_dependencias(agente_origem_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_deps_destino ON agentes_dependencias(agente_destino_id);

-- ============================================
-- TABELA: metricas_agentes (monitoramento de performance)
-- ============================================
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS metricas_agentes (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    
    -- Relacionamento
    agente_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES agentes(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    
    -- Métricas de performance
    tempo_resposta_medio DECIMAL(10, 3) DEFAULT 0,
    taxa_sucesso DECIMAL(5, 2) DEFAULT 0,
    total_execucoes INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_erros INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Métricas de custo
    custo_total DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    custo_medio_por_exec DECIMAL(10, 6) DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Janela temporal
    periodo_inicio TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    periodo_fim TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE NOT NULL,
    
    -- Agregação
    granularidade VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'hora',
    
    -- Timestamps
    calculado_em TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Constraints
    CONSTRAINT check_granularidade CHECK (granularidade IN ('minuto', 'hora', 'dia', 'semana', 'mes')),
    CONSTRAINT check_periodo CHECK (periodo_fim > periodo_inicio)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_metricas_agente_id ON metricas_agentes(agente_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_metricas_periodo ON metricas_agentes(periodo_inicio, periodo_fim);
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX idx_metricas_agregacao ON metricas_agentes(agente_id, periodo_inicio, periodo_fim, granularidade);

-- ============================================
-- FUNÇÕES E TRIGGERS
-- ============================================

-- Função para atualizar o campo atualizado_em automaticamente
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION atualizar_timestamp()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.atualizado_em = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- Triggers para atualização automática de timestamp
CREATE TRIGGER trigger_atualizar_agentes
    BEFORE UPDATE ON agentes
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE FUNCTION atualizar_timestamp();

CREATE TRIGGER trigger_atualizar_configuracoes
    BEFORE UPDATE ON configuracoes_sistema
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE FUNCTION atualizar_timestamp();

-- Função para calcular checksum de migração
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION calcular_checksum_migracao(sql_content TEXT)
RETURNS VARCHAR(64) AS $$
BEGIN
    RETURN encode(digest(sql_content, 'sha256'), 'hex');
END;
$$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

-- ============================================
-- MIGRAÇÃO INICIAL V1.0.0
-- ============================================

-- Script de migração inicial
INSERT INTO migracoes (versao, nome, descricao, aplicada, aplicada_em, checksum) 
VALUES (
    '1.0.0',
    'Schema Inicial DIYAPP V10',
    'Criação das tabelas principais: agentes, logs_execucao, configuracoes_sistema, migracoes, agentes_dependencias, metricas_agentes',
    TRUE,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    'e3b0c44298fc1c149afbf4c8996fb92427ae41e4649b934ca495991b7852b855' -- SHA-256 de string vazia para migração inicial
);

-- ============================================
-- CONFIGURAÇÕES INICIAIS DO SISTEMA
-- ============================================

-- Configurações padrão do sistema
INSERT INTO configuracoes_sistema (chave, valor, tipo, categoria, descricao, sensivel, editavel) VALUES
-- Configurações de LLM
('llm.provedor_padrao', '"openai"', 'string', 'llm', 'Provedor de LLM padrão', FALSE, TRUE),

    '{"permissoes": ["orquestrar_agentes", "monitorar_sistema", "escalar_recursos"], "timeout": 60000, "retry_policy": {"max_attempts": 3, "backoff_factor": 1.5}}',
    0.3,
    4000,
    'gpt-4',
    TRUE,
    TRUE,
    'sistema',
    'sistema'

-- ============================================
-- VIEWS PARA CONSULTA
-- ============================================

-- View para dashboard de agentes
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW view_dashboard_agentes AS
SELECT 
    a.id,
    a.nome,
    a.slug,
    a.versao,
    a.ativo,
    a.modo_hive,
    a.criado_em,
    a.atualizado_em,
    COUNT(DISTINCT l.id) as total_execucoes,
    COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN l.status = 'erro' THEN l.id END) as total_erros,
    COALESCE(AVG(l.duracao_ms), 0) as tempo_resposta_medio,
    COALESCE(SUM(l.custo_total), 0) as custo_total
FROM agentes a
LEFT JOIN logs_execucao l ON a.id = l.agente_id
GROUP BY a.id, a.nome, a.slug, a.versao, a.ativo, a.modo_hive, a.criado_em, a.atualizado_em;

-- View para métricas do sistema
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW view_metricas_sistema AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('hour', l.iniciado_em) as periodo,
    COUNT(*) as total_execucoes,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN l.status = 'sucesso' THEN 1 END) as execucoes_sucesso,
    COUNT(CASE WHEN l.status = 'erro' THEN 1 END) as execucoes_erro,
    AVG(l.duracao_ms) as tempo_resposta_medio,
    SUM(l.tokens_entrada + l.tokens_saida) as total_tokens,
    SUM(l.custo_total) as custo_total
FROM logs_execucao l
WHERE l.iniciado_em >= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP - INTERVAL '24 hours'
GROUP BY DATE_TRUNC('hour', l.iniciado_em)
ORDER BY periodo DESC;

-- ============================================
-- ÍNDICES ADICIONAIS PARA PERFORMANCE
-- ============================================

-- Índices para queries de relatório
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_periodo_agente ON logs_execucao(agente_id, iniciado_em DESC);
CREATE INDEX idx_logs_custo ON logs_execucao(custo_total DESC) WHERE custo_total > 0;

-- Índice para configurações por tipo
CREATE INDEX idx_config_tipo_valor ON configuracoes_sistema(tipo, chave);

-- ============================================
-- SCRIPT DE VALIDAÇÃO DO SCHEMA
-- ============================================

DO $$
DECLARE
    tabelas_esperadas TEXT[] := ARRAY['agentes', 'logs_execucao', 'configuracoes_sistema', 'migracoes', 'agentes_dependencias', 'metricas_agentes'];
    tabela TEXT;
    contagem INTEGER;
BEGIN
    RAISE NOTICE 'Validando schema do banco de dados...';
    
    FOR i IN 1..array_length(tabelas_esperadas, 1) LOOP
        tabela := tabelas_esperadas[i];
        EXECUTE format('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_name = %L', tabela) INTO contagem;
        
        IF contagem = 0 THEN
            RAISE EXCEPTION 'Tabela % não foi criada', tabela;
        ELSE
            RAISE NOTICE '✓ Tabela % criada com sucesso', tabela;
        END IF;
    END LOOP;
    
    -- Verificar migração inicial
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO contagem FROM migracoes WHERE versao = '1.0.0' AND aplicada = TRUE;
    IF contagem =

## 2. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis-data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  redis-commander:
    image: rediscommander/redis-commander:latest
    container_name: diyapp-redis-commander
    environment:
      - REDIS_HOSTS=local:redis:6379
    ports:
      - "8081:8081"
    depends_on:
      - redis
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

  orchestrator:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-orchestrator
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
      - "3001:3001"
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - ORCHESTRATOR_PORT=3000
      - SOCKET_PORT=3001
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./public:/app/public
    depends_on:
      - redis
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  agent-aiops:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-agent-aiops
    environment:
      - NODE_ENV=production
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - AGENT_TYPE=AI_OPS
      - AGENT_ID=aiops-${HOSTNAME}
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    depends_on:
      - redis
      - orchestrator
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

    restart: unless-stopped

    build: .

    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    depends_on:
      - redis
      - orchestrator
    networks:
      - diyapp-network

## 3. Dockerfile

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Install dependencies
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Create logs directory
RUN mkdir -p /app/logs

# Expose ports
EXPOSE 3000 3001

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "const http = require('http'); http.get('http://localhost:3000/health', (r) => {if(r.statusCode === 200) process.exit(0); process.exit(1)})"

CMD ["npm", "start"]
```

## 4. Configuração Principal (src/config/index.js)

```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  // Redis Configuration
  redis: {
    url: process.env.REDIS_URL || 'redis://localhost:6379',
    maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
    enableReadyCheck: false,
    retryStrategy: (times) => {
      const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
      return delay;
    }
  },

  // Queue Configuration
  queues: {
    taskQueue: 'diyapp-tasks',
    heartbeatQueue: 'diyapp-heartbeats',
    priorityQueues: {
      high: 'diyapp-tasks-high',
      medium: 'diyapp-tasks-medium',
      low: 'diyapp-tasks-low'
    },
    defaultPriority: 'medium',
    concurrency: parseInt(process.env.QUEUE_CONCURRENCY) || 5,
    stalledInterval: 30000, // 30 seconds
    removeOnComplete: {
      age: 3600, // Keep completed jobs for 1 hour
      count: 1000 // Keep last 1000 jobs
    },
    removeOnFail: {
      age: 24 * 3600 // Keep failed jobs for 24 hours
    }
  },

  // Agent Configuration
  agents: {
    heartbeatInterval: 10000, // 10 seconds
    heartbeatTimeout: 30000, // 30 seconds
    maxAgentsPerType: 10,
    agentTypes: ['AI_OPS', 'LLM_SPECIALIST', 'QA_SPECIALIST', 'SRE', 'PM']
  },

  // Server Configuration
  server: {
    port: parseInt(process.env.ORCHESTRATOR_PORT) || 3000,
    socketPort: parseInt(process.env.SOCKET_PORT) || 3001,
    rateLimit: {
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
      max: 100 // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
    }
  },

  // Logging Configuration
  logging: {
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    directory: process.env.LOG_DIR || './logs',
    maxFiles: '14d', // Keep logs for 14 days
    maxSize: '20m'
  },

  // Monitoring Configuration
  monitoring: {
    metricsInterval: 60000, // 1 minute
    alertThresholds: {
      queueLength: 1000,
      agentTimeout: 5,
      errorRate: 0.05 // 5%
    }
  }
};

module.exports = config;
```

## 5. Logger Estruturado (src/monitoring/logger.js)

```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const DailyRotateFile = require('winston-daily-rotate-file');
const config = require('../config');

// Define log format
const logFormat = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss.SSS' }),
  winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
  winston.format.json()
);

// Create transports
const transports = [
  // Console transport for development
  new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize(),
      winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message, ...meta }) => {
        return `${timestamp} [${level}]: ${message} ${Object.keys(meta).length ? JSON.stringify(meta) : ''}`;
      })
    ),
    level: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'info' : 'debug'
  }),
  
  // Daily rotate file transport for structured logs
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: `${config.logging.directory}/orchestrator-%DATE%.log`,
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    zippedArchive: true,
    maxSize: config.logging.maxSize,
    maxFiles: config.logging.maxFiles,
    format: logFormat,
    level: config.logging.level
  }),
  
  // Error log file
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: `${config.logging.directory}/error-%DATE%.log`,
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    zippedArchive: true,
    maxSize: config.logging.maxSize,
    maxFiles: config.logging.maxFiles,
    format: logFormat,
    level: 'error'
  })
];

// Create logger instance
const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: config.logging.level,
  format: logFormat,
  transports,
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-orchestrator' }
});

// Agent-specific logger
class AgentLogger {
  constructor(agentId, agentType) {
    this.agentId = agentId;
    this.agentType = agentType;
  }

  info(message, meta = {}) {
    logger.info(message, {
      agentId: this.agentId,
      agentType: this.agentType,
      ...meta
    });
  }

  debug(message, meta = {}) {
    logger.debug(message, {
      agentId: this.agentId,
      agentType: this.agentType,
      ...meta
    });
  }

  warn(message, meta = {}) {
    logger.warn(message, {
      agentId: this.agentId,
      agentType: this.agentType,
      ...meta
    });
  }

  error(message, error = null, meta = {}) {
    logger.error(message, {
      agentId: this.agentId,
      agentType: this.agentType,
      error: error ? {
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
        code: error.code
      } : null,
      ...meta
    });
  }

  // Task execution logging
  logTaskStart(taskId, taskType, priority) {
    this.info('Task execution started', {
      taskId,
      taskType,
      priority,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }

  logTaskComplete(taskId, taskType, duration, result) {
    this.info('Task execution completed', {
      taskId,
      taskType,
      duration,
      resultSummary: typeof result === 'object' ? 
        { type: 'object', keys: Object.keys(result) } : 
        { type: typeof result, value: String(result).substring(0, 100) }
    });
  }

  logTaskError(taskId, taskType, error, retryCount) {
    this.error('Task execution failed', error, {
      taskId,
      taskType,
      retryCount
    });
  }

  // Heartbeat logging
  logHeartbeat(status, metrics = {}) {
    this.debug('Heartbeat sent', {
      status,
      metrics,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
}

// Orchestrator logger
class OrchestratorLogger {
  static logQueueMetrics(queueName, metrics) {
    logger.info('Queue metrics', {
      queueName,
      ...metrics,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }

  static logAgentStatus(agentId, agentType, status, details = {}) {
    logger.info('Agent status update', {
      agentId,
      agentType,
      status,
      ...details,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }

  static logTaskDistribution(taskId, agentId, queueName, priority) {
    logger.info('Task distributed', {
      taskId,
      agentId,
      queueName,
      priority,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }

  static logSystemAlert(alertType, severity, message, data = {}) {
    const logMethod = severity === 'critical' ? 'error' : 
                     severity === 'warning' ? 'warn' : 'info';
    
    logger[logMethod](`System alert: ${message}`, {
      alertType,
      severity,
      ...data,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
}

module.exports = {
  logger,
  AgentLogger,
  OrchestratorLogger
};
```

## 6. Cliente Redis (src/utils/redis-client.js)

```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const config = require('../config');
const { logger } = require('../monitoring/logger');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = null;
    this.subscriber = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.connectionAttempts = 0;
    this.maxConnectionAttempts = 10;
  }

  async connect() {
    try {
      // Create main client
      this.client = new Redis(config.redis.url, {
        maxRetriesPerRequest: config.redis.maxRetriesPerRequest,
        enableReadyCheck: config.redis.enableReadyCheck,
        retryStrategy: config.redis.retryStrategy
      });

      // Create subscriber client for pub/sub
      this.subscriber = new Redis(config.redis.url);

      // Setup event listeners
      this.setupEventListeners();

      // Test connection
      await this.client.ping();
      this.isConnected = true;
      this.connectionAttempts = 0;
      
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
      return this.client;
    } catch (error) {
      this.connectionAttempts++;
      logger.error('Failed to connect to Redis', error);
      
      if (this.connectionAttempts < this.maxConnectionAttempts) {
        const delay = Math.min(this.connectionAttempts * 1000, 5000);
        logger.info(`Retrying connection in ${delay}ms...`);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
        return this.connect();
      }
      
      throw new Error(`Failed to connect to Redis after ${this.maxConnectionAttempts} attempts`);
    }
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis client connecting...');
    });

    this.client.on('ready', () => {
      logger.info('Redis client ready');
      this.isConnected = true;
    });

    this.client.on('error', (error) => {
      logger.error('Redis client error', error);
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('close', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis client connection closed');
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('reconnecting', (delay) => {
      logger.info(`Redis client reconnecting in ${delay}ms`);
    });

    this.client.on('end', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis client connection ended');
      this.isConnected = false;
    });
  }

  async disconnect() {
    try {
      if (this.client) {
        await this.client.quit();
      }
      if (this.subscriber) {
        await this.subscriber.quit();
      }
      logger.info('Redis clients disconnected');
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Error disconnecting Redis clients', error);
    }
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        return { status: 'disconnected', message: 'Redis client not

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
```yaml
# docker-compose.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # PostgreSQL Database
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-changeme}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-db:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user -d diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
      start_period: 30s
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Redis Cache
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --requirepass ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-redispass}
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "--raw", "incr", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Main Application
  app:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    container_name: diyapp-core
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DB_HOST: postgres
      DB_PORT: 5432
      DB_NAME: diyapp
      DB_USER: diyapp_user
      DB_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD:-changeme}
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      REDIS_PORT: 6379
      REDIS_PASSWORD: ${REDIS_PASSWORD:-redispass}
      PROMETHEUS_METRICS_PORT: 9091
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
      - "9091:9091"  # Prometheus metrics endpoint
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
      - ./uploads:/app/uploads
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped
    labels:
      - "prometheus.scrape=true"
      - "prometheus.port=9091"
      - "prometheus.path=/metrics"

  # Prometheus Monitoring
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: diyapp-prometheus
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/console_templates'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=30d'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Grafana Dashboard
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: diyapp-grafana
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD:-admin}
      GF_INSTALL_PLUGINS: grafana-piechart-panel
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
      - ./grafana/dashboards:/var/lib/grafana/dashboards
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    depends_on:
      - prometheus
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Loki Log Aggregation
  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:latest
    container_name: diyapp-loki
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml
    ports:
      - "3100:3100"
    volumes:
      - loki_data:/loki
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Promtail Log Collector
  promtail:
    image: grafana/promtail:latest
    container_name: diyapp-promtail
    volumes:
      - ./promtail/promtail-config.yml:/etc/promtail/config.yml
      - ./logs:/var/log/app
      - /var/log:/var/log/host
    command: -config.file=/etc/promtail/config.yml
    depends_on:
      - loki
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Node Exporter for System Metrics
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:latest
    container_name: diyapp-node-exporter
    volumes:
      - /proc:/host/proc:ro
      - /sys:/host/sys:ro
      - /:/rootfs:ro
    command:
      - '--path.procfs=/host/proc'
      - '--path.rootfs=/rootfs'
      - '--path.sysfs=/host/sys'
      - '--collector.filesystem.mount-points-exclude=^/(sys|proc|dev|host|etc)($$|/)'
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    networks:
      - diyapp-network
    restart: unless-stopped

networks:
  diyapp-network:
    driver: bridge
    name: diyapp-network

  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  redis_data:
    driver: local
  prometheus_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local
  loki_data:
    driver: local

  CMD node healthcheck.js || exit 1

```javascript
// src/monitoring/metrics.js
const promClient = require('prom-client');
const responseTime = require('response-time');

// Create Registry
const register = new promClient.Registry();
promClient.collectDefaultMetrics({ register });

// Custom Metrics
const httpRequestDurationMicroseconds = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of HTTP requests in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.3, 0.5, 0.7, 1, 3, 5, 7, 10]
});

const httpRequestsTotal = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'http_requests_total',
  help: 'Total number of HTTP requests',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code']
});

const databaseQueryDuration = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'database_query_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of database queries in seconds',
  labelNames: ['operation', 'table'],
  buckets: [0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
});

const redisCommandDuration = new promClient.Histogram({
  name: 'redis_command_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Duration of Redis commands in seconds',
  labelNames: ['command'],
  buckets: [0.001, 0.005, 0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5]
});

const activeUsersGauge = new promClient.Gauge({
  name: 'active_users',
  help: 'Number of active users'
});

const errorCounter = new promClient.Counter({
  name: 'application_errors_total',
  help: 'Total number of application errors',
  labelNames: ['type', 'endpoint']
});

// Register metrics
register.registerMetric(httpRequestDurationMicroseconds);
register.registerMetric(httpRequestsTotal);
register.registerMetric(databaseQueryDuration);
register.registerMetric(redisCommandDuration);
register.registerMetric(activeUsersGauge);
register.registerMetric(errorCounter);

// Middleware for HTTP metrics
const metricsMiddleware = responseTime((req, res, time) => {
  const route = req.route?.path || req.path;
  httpRequestDurationMicroseconds
    .labels(req.method, route, res.statusCode)
    .observe(time / 1000);
  
  httpRequestsTotal
    .labels(req.method, route, res.statusCode)
    .inc();
});

// Health check metrics
const healthCheckGauge = new promClient.Gauge({
  name: 'service_health',
  help: 'Health status of the service (1 = healthy, 0 = unhealthy)',
  labelNames: ['service']
});

// Database connection metrics
const dbConnectionsGauge = new promClient.Gauge({
  name: 'database_connections',
  help: 'Number of active database connections',
  labelNames: ['state']
});

// Redis connection metrics
const redisConnectionsGauge = new promClient.Gauge({
  name: 'redis_connections',
  help: 'Number of active Redis connections'
});

module.exports = {
  register,
  metricsMiddleware,
  httpRequestDurationMicroseconds,
  httpRequestsTotal,
  databaseQueryDuration,
  redisCommandDuration,
  activeUsersGauge,
  errorCounter,
  healthCheckGauge,
  dbConnectionsGauge,
  redisConnectionsGauge
};
```

```javascript
// src/monitoring/health.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const redis = require('redis');
const { healthCheckGauge } = require('./metrics');

class HealthChecker {
  constructor() {
    this.checks = [];
    this.dbPool = null;
    this.redisClient = null;
  }

  addDatabaseCheck(pool) {
    this.dbPool = pool;
    this.checks.push({
      name: 'database',
      check: async () => {
        try {
          const result = await pool.query('SELECT 1 as healthy');
          return result.rows[0].healthy === 1;
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Database health check failed:', error);
          return false;
        }
      }
    });
  }

  addRedisCheck(client) {
    this.redisClient = client;
    this.checks.push({
      name: 'redis',
      check: async () => {
        try {
          const pong = await client.ping();
          return pong === 'PONG';
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Redis health check failed:', error);
          return false;
        }
      }
    });
  }

  addDiskSpaceCheck() {
    this.checks.push({
      name: 'disk_space',
      check: async () => {
        try {
          const checkDiskSpace = require('check-disk-space').default;
          const diskSpace = await checkDiskSpace('/');
          const freePercentage = (diskSpace.free / diskSpace.size) * 100;
          return freePercentage > 10; // At least 10% free space
        } catch (error) {
          console.error('Disk space check failed:', error);
          return false;
        }
      }
    });
  }

  async runChecks() {
    const results = {};
    let allHealthy = true;

    for (const check of this.checks) {
      try {
        const isHealthy = await check.check();
        results[check.name] = isHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy';
        healthCheckGauge.labels(check.name).set(isHealthy ? 1 : 0);
        
        if (!isHealthy) {
          allHealthy = false;
        }
      } catch (error) {
        results[check.name] = 'error';
        healthCheckGauge.labels(check.name).set(0);
        allHealthy = false;
      }
    }

    return {
      status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'unhealthy',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      checks: results
    };
  }
}

const healthChecker = new HealthChecker();

// Health endpoints
router.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  const health = await healthChecker.runChecks();
  res.status(health.status === 'healthy' ? 200 : 503).json(health);
});

router.get('/health/live', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'live',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  });
});

router.get('/health/ready', async (req, res) => {
  const health = await healthChecker.runChecks();
  if (health.status === 'healthy') {
    res.status(200).json({
      status: 'ready',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  } else {
    res.status(503).json({
      status: 'not_ready',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      failing: Object.entries(health.checks)
        .filter(([_, status]) => status !== 'healthy')
        .map(([name]) => name)
    });
  }
});

module.exports = {
  router,
  HealthChecker,
  healthChecker
};
```

```javascript
// src/monitoring/logging.js
const winston = require('winston');
const { LokiTransport } = require('winston-loki');
const path = require('path');

const logDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../logs');

const customFormat = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.timestamp({ format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss' }),
  winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
  winston.format.splat(),
  winston.format.json()
);

const consoleFormat = winston.format.combine(
  winston.format.colorize(),
  winston.format.timestamp({ format: 'HH:mm:ss' }),
  winston.format.printf(({ timestamp, level, message, ...meta }) => {
    let metaStr = '';
    if (Object.keys(meta).length > 0) {
      metaStr = ` ${JSON.stringify(meta)}`;
    }
    return `[${timestamp}] ${level}: ${message}${metaStr}`;
  })
);

const transports = [
  new winston.transports.File({
    filename: path.join(logDir, 'error.log'),
    level: 'error',
    maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
    maxFiles: 5
  }),
  new winston.transports.File({
    filename: path.join(logDir, 'combined.log'),
    maxsize: 5242880,
    maxFiles: 5
  })
];

// Add Loki transport if configured
if (process.env.LOKI_HOST) {
  transports.push(new LokiTransport({
    host: process.env.LOKI_HOST,
    labels: { 
      app: 'diyapp',
      environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
      instance: process.env.HOSTNAME || 'local'
    },
    json: true,
    format: customFormat,
    level: 'info',
    replaceTimestamp: true,
    onConnectionError: (err) => console.error('Loki connection error:', err)
  }));
}

// Add console transport in development
if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  transports.push(new winston.transports.Console({
    format: consoleFormat
  }));
}

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: customFormat,
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp' },
  transports,
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(logDir, 'exceptions.log') 
    })
  ],
  rejectionHandlers: [
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(logDir, 'rejections.log') 
    })
  ]
});

// Request logging middleware
const requestLogger = (req, res, next) => {
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    logger.info('HTTP Request', {
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration: `${duration}ms`,
      userAgent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip,
      userId: req.user?.id || 'anonymous'
    });
  });
  
  next();
};

// Error logging middleware
const errorLogger = (err, req, res, next) => {
  logger.error('Unhandled Error', {
    error: err.message,
    stack: err.stack,
    method: req.method,
    url: req.url,
    userId: req.user?.id || 'anonymous',
    ip: req.ip
  });
  
  next(err);
};

module.exports = {
  logger,
  requestLogger,
  errorLogger
};
```
